<table class="box-Expand_language plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-notice" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><span typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Translation_to_zh_arrow.svg/50px-Translation_to_zh_arrow.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="17" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Translation_to_zh_arrow.svg/75px-Translation_to_zh_arrow.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Translation_to_zh_arrow.svg/100px-Translation_to_zh_arrow.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="60" data-file-height="20" /></span></span></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><span class="mbox-text-span">此条目<b>可参照<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Information_theory" class="extiw" title="en:Information theory">英语维基百科</a>相应条目来扩充</b>。<span class="hide-when-compact"></span> <small class="date-container"><i>(<span class="date">2019年10月28日</span>)</i></small><span class="hide-when-compact"><br /><small>若您熟悉来源语言和主题，请协助<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E7%BF%BB%E8%AF%91%E5%AE%88%E5%88%99" class="mw-redirect" title="Wikipedia:翻译守则">参考外语维基百科扩充条目</a>。请勿直接提交机械翻译，也不要翻译不可靠、低品质内容。依<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E5%9C%A8%E7%BB%B4%E5%9F%BA%E7%99%BE%E7%A7%91%E5%86%85%E5%A4%8D%E5%88%B6%E5%86%85%E5%AE%B9" title="Wikipedia:在维基百科内复制内容">版权协议</a>，译文需<a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E7%B7%A8%E8%BC%AF%E6%91%98%E8%A6%81#翻譯文章" title="Wikipedia:编辑摘要">在编辑摘要注明来源</a>，或于讨论页顶部标记<code>{{<a href="/wiki/Template:Translated_page" title="Template:Translated page">Translated page</a>}}</code>标签。</small></span><span class="hide-when-compact"></span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<div id="noteTA-9a130447" class="noteTA"><div class="noteTA-group"><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="Communication"></div><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="IT"></div><div data-noteta-group-source="module" data-noteta-group="Math"></div></div><div class="noteTA-local"><div data-noteta-code="zh-hans:检验;zh-hant:檢定"></div></div></div>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable"><span typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:%E6%B6%88%E6%AD%A7%E4%B9%89" title="Wikipedia:消歧义"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Confusion_grey.svg/24px-Confusion_grey.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="18" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Confusion_grey.svg/36px-Confusion_grey.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Confusion_grey.svg/48px-Confusion_grey.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="260" data-file-height="200" /></a></span><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r74069148">body:not(.skin-minerva) .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.mobile{display:none}body.skin-minerva .mw-parser-output .ifmobile>.nomobile{display:inherit;display:initial}</style><span class="ifmobile"><span class="nomobile">&#160;&#160;</span><span class="mobile"></span></span><b>提示</b>：此条目的主题不是<b><a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E5%AD%A6" class="mw-redirect" title="信息学">信息学</a></b>。</div>
<div role="navigation" aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">
<ul style="display:table;box-sizing:border-box;padding:0.1em;max-width:175px;background:#f9f9f9;font-size:85%;line-height:110%;font-weight:bold">
<li style="display:table-row"><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center"><span class="noviewer" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Nuvola_apps_kcmprocessor.png" class="mw-file-description"><img alt="信息技术" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Nuvola_apps_kcmprocessor.png/28px-Nuvola_apps_kcmprocessor.png" decoding="async" width="28" height="28" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Nuvola_apps_kcmprocessor.png/42px-Nuvola_apps_kcmprocessor.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/50/Nuvola_apps_kcmprocessor.png/56px-Nuvola_apps_kcmprocessor.png 2x" data-file-width="128" data-file-height="128" /></a></span></span><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em 0.2em 0.2em 0.3em;vertical-align:middle"><a href="/wiki/Portal:%E8%B3%87%E8%A8%8A%E7%A7%91%E6%8A%80" title="Portal:信息技术">信息技术主题</a></span></li></ul></div>
<p><b>信息论</b>（英语：<span lang="en">information theory</span>）是<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%94%E7%94%A8%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="应用数学">应用数学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E5%AD%90%E5%AD%B8" class="mw-redirect" title="电子学">电子学</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6" title="计算机科学">计算机科学</a>的一个分支，涉及<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF" title="信息">信息</a>的量化、存储和通信等。信息论是由<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E5%8A%B3%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E9%A6%99%E5%86%9C" title="克劳德·香农">克劳德·香农</a>发展，用来找出<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E5%8F%B7%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86" title="信号处理">信号处理</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E9%80%9A%E4%BF%A1" title="通信">通信</a>操作的基本限制，如<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E5%8E%8B%E7%BC%A9" title="数据压缩">数据压缩</a>、可靠的存储和数据<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B5%E4%BF%A1" title="电信">传输</a>等。自创立以来，它已拓展应用到许多其他领域，包括统计推断、<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80%E5%A4%84%E7%90%86" title="自然语言处理">自然语言处理</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E7%A0%81%E5%AD%A6" title="密码学">密码学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E7%BB%8F%E7%94%9F%E7%89%A9%E5%AD%A6" class="mw-redirect" title="神经生物学">神经生物学</a><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>、进化论<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>和分子编码的功能<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%94%9F%E6%80%81%E5%AD%A6" title="生态学">生态学</a>的模式选择<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>、热物理<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%8F%E5%AD%90%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97" class="mw-redirect" title="量子计算">量子计算</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80%E5%AD%A6" title="语言学">语言学</a>、剽窃检测<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%A8%A1%E5%BC%8F%E8%AF%86%E5%88%AB" title="模式识别">模式识别</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%82%E5%B8%B8%E6%A3%80%E6%B5%8B" title="异常检测">异常检测</a>和其他形式的<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="数据分析">数据分析</a>。<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/%E7%86%B5_(%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA)" title="熵 (信息论)">熵</a>是信息的一个关键度量，通常用一条消息中需要存储或传输一个<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="符号率" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Symbol rate"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%AC%A6%E5%8F%B7%E7%8E%87&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="符号率（页面不存在）">符号</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Symbol_rate" class="extiw" title="en:Symbol rate"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Symbol rate</span></a></span>）</span></span>的平均比特数来表示。熵衡量了预测<a href="/wiki/%E9%9A%8F%E6%9C%BA%E5%8F%98%E9%87%8F" title="随机变量">随机变量</a>的值时涉及到的不确定度的量。例如，指定<a href="/wiki/%E6%93%B2%E7%A1%AC%E5%B9%A3" title="掷硬币">掷硬币</a>的结果（两个等可能的结果）比指定掷骰子的结果（六个等可能的结果）所提供的信息量更少（熵更少）。
</p><p>信息论将信息的传递作为一种统计现象来考虑，给出了估算通信信道容量的方法。信息传输和信息压缩是信息论研究中的两大领域。这两个方面又由<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E5%99%AA%E4%BF%A1%E9%81%93%E7%BC%96%E7%A0%81%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="有噪信道编码定理">信道编码定理</a>、<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%BA%90%EF%BC%8D%E4%BF%A1%E9%81%93%E9%9A%94%E7%A6%BB%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="信源－信道隔离定理（页面不存在）">信源－信道隔离定理</a>相互联系。
</p><p>信息论的基本内容的应用包括<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E6%8D%9F%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E5%8E%8B%E7%BC%A9" title="无损数据压缩">无损数据压缩</a>（如<a href="/wiki/ZIP%E6%A0%BC%E5%BC%8F" title="ZIP格式">ZIP文件</a>）、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E6%8D%9F%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E5%8E%8B%E7%BC%A9" title="有损数据压缩">有损数据压缩</a>（如<a href="/wiki/MP3" title="MP3">MP3</a>和<a href="/wiki/JPEG" title="JPEG">JPEG</a>）、<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E9%81%93%E5%AE%B9%E9%87%8F" title="信道容量">信道编码</a>（如<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%97%E7%94%A8%E6%88%B7%E7%BA%BF%E8%B7%AF" title="数字用户线路">数字用户线路</a>（<span lang="en">DSL</span>））。这个领域处在<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="数学">数学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%BB%9F%E8%AE%A1%E5%AD%A6" title="统计学">统计学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6" title="计算机科学">计算机科学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%89%A9%E7%90%86%E5%AD%A6" title="物理学">物理学</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%A5%9E%E7%BB%8F%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6" title="神经科学">神经科学</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%BB%E6%A9%9F%E5%B7%A5%E7%A8%8B%E5%AD%B8" title="电机工程学">电机工程学</a>的交叉点上。信息论对<a href="/wiki/%E8%88%AA%E6%B5%B7%E5%AE%B6%E8%A8%88%E7%95%AB" title="航海家项目">航海家</a>深空探测任务的成败、<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%89%E7%9B%98" class="mw-redirect" title="光盘">光盘</a>的发明、<a href="/wiki/%E6%89%8B%E6%9C%BA" class="mw-redirect" title="手机">手机</a>的可行性、<a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E8%81%94%E7%BD%91" title="互联网">互联网</a>的发展、<a href="/wiki/%E8%AF%AD%E8%A8%80%E5%AD%A6" title="语言学">语言学</a>和人类感知的研究、对<a href="/wiki/%E9%BB%91%E6%B4%9E" title="黑洞">黑洞</a>的了解，以及许多其他领域都影响深远。信息论的重要子领域有<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E5%8E%8B%E7%BC%A9" title="数据压缩">信源编码</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%89%8D%E5%90%91%E9%8C%AF%E8%AA%A4%E6%9B%B4%E6%AD%A3" title="前向纠错">信道编码</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E6%B0%8F%E5%A4%8D%E6%9D%82%E6%80%A7" title="柯氏复杂性">算法复杂性理论</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E7%AE%97%E6%B3%95%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA" title="算法信息论">算法信息论</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%B3%87%E8%A8%8A%E7%90%86%E8%AB%96%E5%AE%89%E5%85%A8%E6%80%A7" title="信息论安全性">信息论安全性</a>和<a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E5%BA%A6%E9%87%8F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="信息度量（页面不存在）">信息度量</a>等。
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span id=".E7.AE.80.E8.BF.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="简述">简述</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：简述"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>信息论的主要内容可以类比人类最广泛的交流手段——语言来阐述。
</p><p>一种简洁的语言（以<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%B1%E8%AF%AD" title="英语">英语</a>为例）通常有两个重要特点：
首先，最常用的词（比如"a"、"the"、"I"）应该比不太常用的词（比如"benefit"、"generation"、"mediocre"）要短一些；其次，如果句子的某一部分被漏听或者由于<a href="/wiki/%E5%99%AA%E5%A3%B0" class="mw-redirect" title="噪声">噪声</a>干扰（比如一辆车辆疾驰而过）而被误听，听者应该仍然可以抓住句子的大概意思。而如果把电子<a href="/wiki/%E9%80%9A%E4%BF%A1%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F" title="通信系统">通信系统</a>比作一种语言的话，这种<a href="/wiki/%E5%81%A5%E5%A3%AE%E6%80%A7_(%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%9C%BA%E7%A7%91%E5%AD%A6)" title="健壮性 (计算机科学)">健壮性</a>（<span lang="en">robustness</span>）是不可或缺的。将健壮性引入通信是通过<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E9%81%93%E7%BC%96%E7%A0%81" title="信道编码">信道编码</a>完成的。<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E6%BA%90%E7%BC%96%E7%A0%81" class="mw-redirect" title="信源编码">信源编码</a>和信道编码是信息论的基本研究课题。
</p><p>注意这些内容同消息的重要性之间是毫不相干的。例如，像“多谢；常来”这样的客套话与像“救命”这样的紧急请求在说起来、或者写起来所花的时间是差不多的，然而明显后者更重要，也更有实在意义。信息论却不考虑一段消息的重要性或内在意义，因为这些是数据的质量的问题而不是数据量（数据的长度）和可读性方面上的问题，后者只是由<a href="/wiki/%E6%A6%82%E7%8E%87" title="概率">概率</a>这一因素单独决定的。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E4.BF.A1.E6.81.AF.E7.9A.84.E5.BA.A6.E9.87.8F"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="信息的度量">信息的度量</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：信息的度量"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E4.BF.A1.E6.81.AF.E7.86.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="信息熵">信息熵</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：信息熵"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>美国数学家<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%8B%E5%8A%B3%E5%BE%B7%C2%B7%E9%A6%99%E5%86%9C" title="克劳德·香农">克劳德·香农</a>被称为“信息论之父”。人们通常将香农于1948年10月发表于《<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="贝尔系统技术学报" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Bell System Technical Journal"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B4%9D%E5%B0%94%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%9F%E6%8A%80%E6%9C%AF%E5%AD%A6%E6%8A%A5&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="贝尔系统技术学报（页面不存在）">贝尔系统技术学报</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bell_System_Technical_Journal" class="extiw" title="en:Bell System Technical Journal"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Bell System Technical Journal</span></a></span>）</span></span>》上的论文《<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="通信的数学理论" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="A Mathematical Theory of Communication"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%80%9A%E4%BF%A1%E7%9A%84%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E7%90%86%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="通信的数学理论（页面不存在）">通信的数学理论</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/A_Mathematical_Theory_of_Communication" class="extiw" title="en:A Mathematical Theory of Communication"><span lang="en" dir="auto">A Mathematical Theory of Communication</span></a></span>）</span></span>》作为现代信息论研究的开端。这一文章部分基于<a href="/wiki/%E5%93%88%E9%87%8C%C2%B7%E5%A5%88%E5%A5%8E%E6%96%AF%E7%89%B9" title="哈里·奈奎斯特">哈里·奈奎斯特</a>和<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="拉尔夫·哈特利" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Ralph Hartley"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%8B%89%E5%B0%94%E5%A4%AB%C2%B7%E5%93%88%E7%89%B9%E5%88%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="拉尔夫·哈特利（页面不存在）">拉尔夫·哈特利</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ralph_Hartley" class="extiw" title="en:Ralph Hartley"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Ralph Hartley</span></a></span>）</span></span>于1920年代先后发表的研究成果。在该文中，香农给出了<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E7%86%B5" class="mw-redirect" title="信息熵">信息熵</a>的定义：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(X)=\mathbb {E} _{X}[I(x)]=\sum _{x\in {\mathcal {X}}}^{}p(x)\log _{2}\left({\frac {1}{p(x)}}\right)}">

<p>其中<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {X}}}">

  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi class="MJX-tex-caligraphic" mathvariant="script">X</mi>
          </mrow>
        </mrow>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\mathcal {X}}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8c7e5461c5286852df4ef652fca7e4b0b63030e9" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.875ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle {\mathcal {X}}}"></span>上的随机变量。信息熵是随机事件不确定性的度量。
</p><p>信息熵与物理学中的<a href="/wiki/%E7%83%AD%E5%8A%9B%E5%AD%A6%E7%86%B5" class="mw-redirect" title="热力学熵">热力学熵</a>有着紧密的联系:
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle S(X)=k_{B}H(X)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>S</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <msub>
          <mi>k</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>B</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S(X)=k_{B}H(X)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/74c1fac0e03d48546eb4f30d57f8a47c1a4ba930" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:16.931ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle S(X)=k_{B}H(X)}"></span></dd></dl>
<p>其中S(X)为热力学熵，H(X)为信息熵，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle k_{B}}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msub>
          <mi>k</mi>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>B</mi>
          </mrow>
        </msub>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle k_{B}}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/70f38f7b73e53fd7b5d9ca64bec3a1438cc0eade" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.691ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle k_{B}}"></span>为<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%A2%E8%8C%B2%E6%9B%BC%E5%B8%B8%E6%95%B8" title="波兹曼常数">波兹曼常数</a>。
事实上这个关系也就是广义的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B3%A2%E8%8C%B2%E6%9B%BC%E7%86%B5%E5%85%AC%E5%BC%8F" title="波兹曼熵公式">波兹曼熵公式</a>，或是在<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E5%88%99%E7%B3%BB%E7%BB%BC" title="正则系综">正则系综</a>内的热力学熵表示式。如此可知，<a href="/wiki/%E7%8E%BB%E5%B0%94%E5%85%B9%E6%9B%BC" class="mw-redirect" title="玻尔兹曼">玻尔兹曼</a>与<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%89%E5%B8%83%E6%96%AF" class="mw-redirect" title="吉布斯">吉布斯</a>在统计物理学中对熵的工作，启发了信息论的熵。
</p><p>信息熵是<a href="/wiki/%E4%BF%A1%E6%BA%90%E7%BC%96%E7%A0%81%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="信源编码定理">信源编码定理</a>中，压缩率的下限。若编码所用的信息量少于信息熵，则一定有信息的损失。香农在<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%A7%E6%95%B0%E5%AE%9A%E5%BE%8B" class="mw-redirect" title="大数定律">大数定律</a>和<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="渐进均分性" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Asymptotic equipartition property"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%B8%90%E8%BF%9B%E5%9D%87%E5%88%86%E6%80%A7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="渐进均分性（页面不存在）">渐进均分性</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Asymptotic_equipartition_property" class="extiw" title="en:Asymptotic equipartition property"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Asymptotic equipartition property</span></a></span>）</span></span>的基础上定义了<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="典型集" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="Typical set"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%85%B8%E5%9E%8B%E9%9B%86&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="典型集（页面不存在）">典型集</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Typical_set" class="extiw" title="en:Typical set"><span lang="en" dir="auto">Typical set</span></a></span>）</span></span>和典型序列。典型集是典型序列的集合。因为一个独立同分布的<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>序列属于由<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>定义的典型集的概率大约为1，所以只需要将属于典型集的无记忆<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>信源序列编为唯一可译码，其他序列随意编码，就可以达到几乎无损失的压缩。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E4.BE.8B.E5.AD.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="例子">例子</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：例子"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>设有一个三个面的骰子，三面分别写有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle 1,2,3}">

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f5fbdaf4e450f3413cfbe25ca0f24e15e6dc6ead" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:5.555ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle 1,2,3}"></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">

<h3><span id=".E8.81.AF.E5.90.88.E7.86.B5.E8.88.87.E6.A2.9D.E4.BB.B6.E7.86.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="聯合熵與條件熵">联合熵与条件熵</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：联合熵与条件熵"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E7%86%B5" title="联合熵">联合熵</a>（<span lang="en">Joint Entropy</span>）由熵的定义出发，计算<a href="/wiki/%E8%81%94%E5%90%88%E5%88%86%E5%B8%83" title="联合分布">联合分布</a>的熵：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=\sum _{x\in {\mathcal {X}}}\sum _{y\in {\mathcal {Y}}}^{}p(x,y)\log \left({\frac {1}{p(x,y)}}\right).}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <munder>
          <mo>&#x2211;<!-- ∑ --></mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mi>x</mi>
            <mo>&#x2208;<!-- ∈ --></mo>
            <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/46d8eadefa1a612877e1744899044b0a84bbdfb8" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -3.338ex; width:40.509ex; height:7.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=\sum _{x\in {\mathcal {X}}}\sum _{y\in {\mathcal {Y}}}^{}p(x,y)\log \left({\frac {1}{p(x,y)}}\right).}"></span></dd></dl>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E6%9D%A1%E4%BB%B6%E7%86%B5" title="条件熵">条件熵</a>（<span lang="en">Conditional Entropy</span>），顾名思义，是以条件概率<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle p(y|x)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3cad17372ea694e639c3881b2b5583632cdaa0ac" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:6.2ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle p(y|x)}"></span>计算：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(Y|X)=\sum _{x\in {\mathcal {X}}}\sum _{y\in {\mathcal {Y}}}^{}p(x,y)\log \left({\frac {1}{p(y|x)}}\right).}">
  <semantics>

              </mrow>
            </mrow>
          </mrow>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

          </mrow>
        </munderover>
        <mi>p</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mi>log</mi>
        <mo>&#x2061;<!-- ⁡ --></mo>
        <mrow>
          <mo>(</mo>
          <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
            <mfrac>
              <mn>1</mn>
              <mrow>
                <mi>p</mi>
                <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
                <mi>y</mi>
                <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
                  <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
                </mrow>
                <mi>x</mi>
                <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
              </mrow>
            </mfrac>
          </mrow>
          <mo>)</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mo>.</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle H(Y|X)=\sum _{x\in {\mathcal {X}}}\sum _{y\in {\mathcal {Y}}}^{}p(x,y)\log \left({\frac {1}{p(y|x)}}\right).}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8a01f19f60eeba6669824e13f9d1aed329a96767" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -3.338ex; width:39.735ex; height:7.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(Y|X)=\sum _{x\in {\mathcal {X}}}\sum _{y\in {\mathcal {Y}}}^{}p(x,y)\log \left({\frac {1}{p(y|x)}}\right).}"></span></dd></dl>
<p>由<a href="/wiki/%E8%B2%9D%E6%B0%8F%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" class="mw-redirect" title="贝叶斯理论">贝叶斯理论</a>，有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle p(x,y)=p(y|x)p(x)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>p</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>p</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>

          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mi>p</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>x</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle p(x,y)=p(y|x)p(x)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/36662171edb972b50ac4297aa7eb2395751b99bb" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; margin-left: -0.089ex; width:20.105ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle p(x,y)=p(y|x)p(x)}"></span>，代入联合熵的定义，可以分离出条件熵，于是得到联合熵与条件熵的关系式:
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=H(X)+H(Y|X)=H(Y)+H(X|Y)=H(Y,X).}">

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=H(X)+H(Y|X)=H(Y)+H(X|Y)=H(Y,X).}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4e5e692f511a7a54f6559ad0e71d5421417cfd8f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:60.989ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=H(X)+H(Y|X)=H(Y)+H(X|Y)=H(Y,X).}"></span></dd></dl>
<h4><span id=".E9.93.BE.E5.BC.8F.E6.B3.95.E5.89.87"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="链式法則">链式法则</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：链式法则"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>可以再对联合熵与条件熵的关系做推广，假设现在有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle n}">

<p>其直观意义如下：假如接收一段数列<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle \{X_{1},X_{2},...,X_{n}\}}">

          </mrow>

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2ad47c14b8a092f182512e76c96638aea6e3bea1" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.979ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X_{2}}"></span>后总信息量为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(X_{1})+H(X_{2}|X_{1})}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>

          </mrow>
        </msub>

      </mstyle>

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle H(X_{1})+H(X_{2}|X_{1})}</annotation>
  </semantics>

  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <msub>

<h3><span id=".E4.BA.92.E4.BF.A1.E6.81.AF"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="互信息">互信息</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：互信息"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%92%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF" title="互信息">互信息</a>（<span lang="en">Mutual Information</span>）是另一有用的信息度量，它是指两个事件集合之间的相关性。两个事件<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Y</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Y}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y}"></span>的互信息定义为：
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle I(X;Y)=H(X)-H(X|Y)=H(X)+H(Y)-H(X,Y)=H(Y)-H(Y|X)=I(Y;X).}">
  <semantics>

        </mrow>

        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>Y</mi>

        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>

<p>其意义为，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">
  <semantics>

        <mi>Y</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Y}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y}"></span>包含<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>的多少信息。在尚未得到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Y</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Y}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y}"></span>之前，对<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle X}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>的不确定性是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(X)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>

      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle H(X)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bd232b6fb5ea803efc1154d2efb0c3fe00a4531b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:5.853ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(X)}"></span>，得到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">

  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>

        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle H(X|Y)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cd2aef35bbe076060f08acfd4a7d314f909ff2c7" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.273ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(X|Y)}"></span>。所以一旦得到<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">

  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>&#x2212;<!-- − --></mo>
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>

        </mrow>

        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4a80bc1290dcba8f1a4ab1dbdf81711a69964f2a" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:16.966ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(X)-H(X|Y)}"></span>的不确定量，这就是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y}">

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/961d67d6b454b4df2301ac571808a3538b3a6d3f" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.171ex; width:1.773ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y}"></span>对<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>X</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>

</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/68baa052181f707c662844a465bfeeb135e82bab" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.98ex; height:2.176ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X}"></span>的信息量。
</p><p>如果<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle X,Y}">
  <semantics>

  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8705438171d938b7f59cd1bfa5b7d99b6afa5cd" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:4.787ex; height:2.509ex;" alt="{\displaystyle X,Y}"></span>互为独立，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=H(X)+H(Y)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>

        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>

    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=H(X)+H(Y)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/41b9cc4a524a355214eafb8883ccde26a88ca9ce" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:26.098ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(X,Y)=H(X)+H(Y)}"></span>，于是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle I(X;Y)=0}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>I</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo>;</mo>
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mn>0</mn>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle I(X;Y)=0}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a23581bf77d5a443737b23f1933bab2d1944075b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:12.029ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle I(X;Y)=0}"></span>。
</p><p>又因为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle H(X|Y)\leq H(X)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
          <mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
        </mrow>
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>&#x2264;<!-- ≤ --></mo>
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle H(X|Y)\leq H(X)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/abdfca47bc7fb81437892bd8fc11e6fb557258d5" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:17.224ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle H(X|Y)\leq H(X)}"></span>，所以
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle I(X;Y)\leq \min(H(X),H(Y)),}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>I</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo>;</mo>
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>&#x2264;<!-- ≤ --></mo>
        <mo movablelimits="true" form="prefix">min</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>,</mo>
        <mi>H</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
        <mo>,</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle I(X;Y)\leq \min(H(X),H(Y)),}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/46efc267dd2bf8aaddd09033f0706890fde40d6b" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:29.731ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle I(X;Y)\leq \min(H(X),H(Y)),}"></span></dd></dl>
<p>其中等号成立条件为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle Y=g(X)}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>Y</mi>
        <mo>=</mo>
        <mi>g</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
        <mi>X</mi>
        <mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle Y=g(X)}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/84fd834147d6175f13477acff6567727265d0000" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:9.777ex; height:2.843ex;" alt="{\displaystyle Y=g(X)}"></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"  alttext="{\displaystyle g}">
  <semantics>
    <mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
      <mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
        <mi>g</mi>
      </mstyle>
    </mrow>
    <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle g}</annotation>
  </semantics>
</math></span><img src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/d3556280e66fe2c0d0140df20935a6f057381d77" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline mw-invert" aria-hidden="true" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.116ex; height:2.009ex;" alt="{\displaystyle g}"></span>是一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%8C%E5%B0%84" title="双射">双射</a>函数。
</p><p>互信息与<span class="ilh-all" data-orig-title="G检验" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-foreign-title="G-test"><span class="ilh-page"><a href="/w/index.php?title=G%E6%A3%80%E9%AA%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="G检验（页面不存在）">G检验</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/G-test" class="extiw" title="en:G-test"><span lang="en" dir="auto">G-test</span></a></span>）</span></span>以及<a href="/wiki/%E7%9A%AE%E7%88%BE%E6%A3%AE%E5%8D%A1%E6%96%B9%E6%AA%A2%E5%AE%9A" title="皮尔逊卡方检验">皮尔森卡方检验</a>有着密切的联系。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.BA.94.E7.94.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="应用">应用</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E4%BF%A1%E6%81%AF%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：应用"><span>编辑</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>信息论被广泛应用在：
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E7%B7%A8%E7%A2%BC%E7%90%86%E8%AB%96" class="mw-redirect" title="编码理论">编码理论</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%86%E7%A0%81%E5%AD%A6" title="密码学">密码学</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E4%BC%A0%E8%BE%93" title="数据传输">数据传输</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E6%8D%AE%E5%8E%8B%E7%BC%A9" title="数据压缩">数据压缩</a></li>
<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%A3%80%E6%B5%8B%E7%90%86%E8%AE%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="检测理论（页面不存在）">检测理论</a></li>
